he spe su ci


Spell    : Summoning Circle

Sphere   : Summoning
Usage    : cast 'summoning circle'
Duration : Varies
Effects  : Creates a summoning circle on the ground

This spell creates a summoning circle on the ground. Casters may use their
own circles to 'summon' players to their location, pretty much like casting
the summon spell.

Details:
- Utility spell which allows the caster to use the 'summon' command to
  attempt to summon people.
- Summon command can only take player names as arguments.
- Has unlimited uses against group and clan members, otherwise each use
  reduces duration.
